<p><strong>74:11</strong> — ذَرۡنِى وَمَنۡ خَلَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>تُ وَحِيدًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:15</strong> — ثُمَّ يَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>طۡ</span>مَعُ أَنۡ أَزِي<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>د</span>َ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:23</strong> — ثُمَّ أَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span>بَرَ وَٱسۡتَكۡبَرَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:27</strong> — وَمَآ أَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span>رَٮٰكَ مَا سَقَرُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:28</strong> — لَا تُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>قِى وَلَا تَذَرُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:33</strong> — وَٱلَّيۡلِ إِذۡ أَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span>بَرَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:34</strong> — وَٱلصُّ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>حِ إِذَآ أَسۡفَرَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:41</strong> — عَنِ ٱلۡمُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>رِمِينَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:44</strong> — وَلَمۡ نَكُ نُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>طۡ</span>عِمُ ٱلۡمِسۡكِينَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>74:56</strong> — وَمَا يَذۡكُرُونَ إِلَّآ أَن يَشَآءَ ٱللَّهُ‌ۚ هُوَ أَهۡلُ ٱلتَّ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>وَىٰ وَأَهۡلُ ٱلۡمَغۡفِرَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:1</strong> — لَآ أُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>سِمُ بِيَوۡمِ ٱلۡقِيَـٰمَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:2</strong> — وَلَآ أُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>سِمُ بِٱلنَّفۡسِ ٱللَّوَّامَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:3</strong> — أَيَحۡسَبُ ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنُ أَلَّن نَّ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>مَعَ عِظَامَهُۥ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:27</strong> — وَقِيلَ مَنۡۜ رَا<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ق</span>ٍ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:28</strong> — وَظَنَّ أَنَّهُ ٱلۡفِرَا<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ق</span>ُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:29</strong> — وَٱلۡتَفَّتِ ٱلسَّاقُ بِٱلسَّا<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ق</span>ِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:30</strong> — إِلَىٰ رَبِّكَ يَوۡمَئِذٍ ٱلۡمَسَا<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ق</span>ُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>75:37</strong> — أَلَمۡ يَكُ نُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>طۡ</span>فَةً مِّن مَّنِىٍّ يُمۡنَىٰ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:2</strong> — إِنَّا خَلَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>نَا ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ مِن نُّ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>طۡ</span>فَةٍ أَمۡشَاجٍ نَّ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>تَلِيهِ فَجَعَلۡنَـٰهُ سَمِيعَۢا بَصِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 3)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:4</strong> — إِنَّآ أَعۡتَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span>نَا لِلۡكَـٰفِرِينَ سَلَـٰسِلَاۡ وَأَغۡلَـٰلاً وَسَعِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:5</strong> — إِنَّ ٱلۡأَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>رَارَ يَشۡرَبُونَ مِن كَأۡسٍ كَانَ مِزَاجُهَا كَافُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:8</strong> — وَيُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>طۡ</span>عِمُونَ ٱلطَّعَامَ عَلَىٰ حُبِّهِۦ مِسۡكِينًا وَيَتِيمًا وَأَسِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:9</strong> — إِنَّمَا نُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>طۡ</span>عِمُكُمۡ لِوَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>هِ ٱللَّهِ لَا نُرِيدُ مِنكُمۡ جَزَآءً وَلَا شُكُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:16</strong> — قَوَارِيرَاۡ مِن فِضَّةٍ قَدَّرُوهَا تَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>دِيرًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:19</strong> — ۞وَيَطُوفُ عَلَيۡهِمۡ وِلۡد<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>نٌ مُّخَلَّدُونَ إِذَا رَأَيۡتَهُمۡ حَسِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>تَهُمۡ لُؤۡلُؤًا مَّنثُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:21</strong> — عَـٰلِيَهُمۡ ثِيَابُ سُندُسٍ خُضۡرٌ وَإِسۡتَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>رَقٌ‌ۖ وَحُلُّوٓاۡ أَسَاوِرَ مِن فِضَّةٍ وَسَقَـٰهُمۡ رَبُّهُمۡ شَرَابًا طَهُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:26</strong> — وَمِنَ ٱلَّيۡلِ فَٱسۡجُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span> لَهُۥ وَسَبِّحۡهُ لَيۡلاً طَوِيلاً <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:28</strong> — نَّحۡنُ خَلَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>نَـٰهُمۡ وَشَدَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span>نَآ أَسۡرَهُمۡ‌ۖ وَإِذَا شِئۡنَا بَدَّلۡنَآ أَمۡثَـٰلَهُمۡ تَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>دِيلاً <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 3)</span></p>
<p><strong>76:31</strong> — يُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span>خِلُ مَن يَشَآءُ فِى رَحۡمَتِهِۦ‌ۚ وَٱلظَّـٰلِمِينَ أَعَدَّ لَهُمۡ عَذَابًا أَلِيمَۢا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:14</strong> — وَمَآ أَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>دۡ</span>رَٮٰكَ مَا يَوۡمُ ٱلۡفَصۡلِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:18</strong> — كَذ<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>لِكَ نَفۡعَلُ بِٱلۡمُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>رِمِينَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:25</strong> — أَلَمۡ نَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>عَلِ ٱلۡأَرۡضَ كِفَاتًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:30</strong> — ٱنطَلِقُوٓاۡ إِلَىٰ ظِلٍّ ذِى ثَلَـٰثِ شُعَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ب</span>ٍ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:31</strong> — لَّا ظَلِيلٍ وَلَا يُغۡنِى مِنَ ٱللَّهَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ب</span>ِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:44</strong> — إِنَّا كَذ<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>لِكَ نَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>زِى ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِينَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>77:46</strong> — كُلُواۡ وَتَمَتَّعُواۡ قَلِيلاً إِنَّكُم مُّ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>رِمُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>78:6</strong> — أَلَمۡ نَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>جۡ</span>عَلِ ٱلۡأَرۡضَ مِهَـٰدًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>78:8</strong> — وَخَلَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>قۡ</span>نَـٰكُمۡ أَزۡو<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>جًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>78:12</strong> — وَبَنَيۡنَا فَوۡقَكُمۡ سَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>عًا شِدَادًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>78:19</strong> — وَفُتِحَتِ ٱلسَّمَآءُ فَكَانَتۡ أَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>و<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>بًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>

<p><strong>111:5</strong> — فِى جِيدِهَا حَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>بۡ</span>لٌ مِّن مَّسَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>د</span>ِۭ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>

<p><strong>113:1</strong> — قُلۡ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلۡفَلَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ق</span>ِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>113:2</strong> — مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>ق</span>َ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
